<div id="review_1247741955" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1247741955" />
    <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie"><img alt="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505392311p2/11641363.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1247741955?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie " href="/user/show/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie">Christine Wallflower &amp; Dark Romance Junkie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11339124-warprize">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=historical">historical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=bossy-guys">bossy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=broody-heroes">broody-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=wishy-washy-shag-scenes">wishy-washy-shag-scenes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11641363-christine-wallflower-dark-romance-junkie?shelf=blah-blah-snore">blah-blah-snore</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1247741955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17823807440810812901"><b>
  <i>"Want to know the best part about being a warlord?" came a hoarse whisper. I bit my lip, puzzled by the question. Keir's mouth curled up slowly into a smile. "I always get what I want."</i>
</b><br/><br/>A bit of an anticlimactic quote since the war lord was in fact not a jerk! All jokes aside I did like this book, it wasn't amazing but there was something about it. I went in expecting a high fantasy romance with some magic and epic world building but aside from a little world building this was more of a roman</span>
  <span id="freeText17823807440810812901" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Want to know the best part about being a warlord?" came a hoarse whisper. I bit my lip, puzzled by the question. Keir's mouth curled up slowly into a smile. "I always get what I want."</i>
</b><br /><br />A bit of an anticlimactic quote since the war lord was in fact not a jerk! All jokes aside I did like this book, it wasn't amazing but there was something about it. I went in expecting a high fantasy romance with some magic and epic world building but aside from a little world building this was more of a romance set in a vague medieval world if that makes any sense.<br /><br />Xylara the heroine, is a healer but most importantly a princess. Her brother Xymund who hates her is the King. When their small kingdom is invaded by barbarians Lara is chosen as the warprize at the war lord's request. Now somethings that annoyed me in this book were the blatant misunderstandings. I won't go into the specifics but basically the story's foundation is that Lara is given as warprize to the War lord to maintain peace between the kingdoms. In my opinion this was a very weak foundation, and the fact that she had the wrong idea about what her role was just plain stupid.<br /><br />I did love Kier and how protective he was of Lara. Marcus's character was also quote entertaining, so was Anna. I loved how Lara managed to win Kier's army over. Like I said there wasn't much magic or adventure. This really was just a romance and the conflicts the couple needed to overcome.<br /><br />I know I always want romance in the books I read but I expected a prophecy or maybe something more significant that just Kier and Lara trying to live happily ever after. I'm sure I'll read the rest of the series at some point but I'm not itching to read the next book right now</span>
  <a data-text-id="17823807440810812901" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3401535260" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8269228144393060199"><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I'm not sure what to say about this. It was not inherently bad, but just not my cup of tea. The writing was bland and a lot of passages were redundant, namely those describing daily tasks and other actions that contributed neither to the plotline, nor to further insights into the characters. It got so boring to the point I wasn't sure whether I was going to finish it. There was just no depth. <br/><br/>The only thing I can say for certain about the protagonist, Xylara, is that she's so selfless i</span>
  <span id="freeText8269228144393060199" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b><br /><br />I'm not sure what to say about this. It was not inherently bad, but just not my cup of tea. The writing was bland and a lot of passages were redundant, namely those describing daily tasks and other actions that contributed neither to the plotline, nor to further insights into the characters. It got so boring to the point I wasn't sure whether I was going to finish it. There was just no depth. <br /><br />The only thing I can say for certain about the protagonist, Xylara, is that she's so selfless it went from admirable to annoying. And trust me, I'm not always asking for a badass heroine who fights for herself and does what she wants, how she wants (these can be just as annoying), but here, a little self-assertion would've made this a little more realistic and bearable. <br /><br />This book is shelved by over a thousand people as a fantasy, but after having read this, I can safely say it's not that. If you're looking for a great fantasy novel with amazing, mind-boggling world-building, this is not it. This is more a historical novel set in the early Middle Ages than anything else. The main theme concerns a clash of traditions and cultural misunderstandings between to peoples. Though the concept is certainly interesting, <i>Warprize</i> does not live up to its potential. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8269228144393060199" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1907403180?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

           <span class="uitext reviewText">Jonetta</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Sunny by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/15582397-phoebe">Phoebe</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1022402-sunny?shelf=a-pnr-uf-fantasy">a-pnr-uf-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1022402-sunny?shelf=a-1-favorites-pnr-uf-fantasy">a-1-favorites-pnr-uf-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1907403180" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1367850896534329786">One of my favorite books as a kid was <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/407813.The_Blue_Sword__Damar___1_' title='The Blue Sword (Damar, #1) by Robin McKinley' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Blue Sword</a> by Robin McKinley. This book has the same feel. I was completely engrossed in the story. It is a great balance between action and character development. I was thoroughly engaged with the characters. Two small things could have made this stronger for me: 1. I would like to know more about Keir and his perspective. I think this was limited because the story is told from a singular point of view, Lara's. 2. As an adult reader, I could have used a</span>
  <span id="freeText1367850896534329786" style="display:none">One of my favorite books as a kid was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/407813.The_Blue_Sword__Damar___1_" title="The Blue Sword (Damar, #1) by Robin McKinley" rel="nofollow noopener">The Blue Sword</a> by Robin McKinley. This book has the same feel. I was completely engrossed in the story. It is a great balance between action and character development. I was thoroughly engaged with the characters. Two small things could have made this stronger for me: 1. I would like to know more about Keir and his perspective. I think this was limited because the story is told from a singular point of view, Lara's. 2. As an adult reader, I could have used a little more romance. I appreciated that this was not necessarily insta-love, but it is not quite clear to me Keir's motivations. Still, a very solid fantasy adventure.</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=fantasy-rom">fantasy-rom</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2478293-zeek?shelf=chick-fantasy">chick-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer216151038" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8590015600399018132">Lara is a healer and, in her eyes, that takes precedence over her royal blood. By simply being who she is, she finds herself sold as war booty to appease a warlord about to overtake her weak brother's kingdom.<br/><br/>And yet still, she is who she is, and her healing ways make her just as beloved by the people in the warlord's camp as she ever was in the Kingdom of Xy. Because she will not compromise her beliefs as a healer, she's about to change two kingdoms, for the better.<br/><br/>Loved every minute of this ch</span>
  <span id="freeText8590015600399018132" style="display:none">Lara is a healer and, in her eyes, that takes precedence over her royal blood. By simply being who she is, she finds herself sold as war booty to appease a warlord about to overtake her weak brother's kingdom.<br /><br />And yet still, she is who she is, and her healing ways make her just as beloved by the people in the warlord's camp as she ever was in the Kingdom of Xy. Because she will not compromise her beliefs as a healer, she's about to change two kingdoms, for the better.<br /><br />Loved every minute of this chick-fantasy. (And guys? This book is <i>so</i> "girls only". You just wont get it. ((two words. War. Lord... but a non threatening one.)) :P) I thought for sure the hero was gonna end up being a shape shifter, I've read so much PNR, but I was wrong, and yet still it was so good. <br /><br />Since it's first person we're not in the heroes head at all but I love that his actions are enough. Same actually could have been said about the heroine even though it <i>was</i> told in her voice. I'll give, She <i>is</i> a bit naive for believing in the bad guy for so long, but I'll forgive her that for her wonderful selflessness and standing up for what she believes in. Plus, her favorite things are her books and helping others. I was so in.<br /><br />The romance is tame but still kept me interested. Personally the "big reveal", as some other reviewer's have called it, really wasnt much of one. What really makes this book work is the Warlord's culture and his desire to merge with the Warprize's very different culture. <br /><br /> <br /><br />Loved. It.</span>

<div id="review_1109327714" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1109327714" />

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=strong-and-kickass-heroines">strong-and-kickass-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=gorgeous-guys">gorgeous-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=ethics-and-society">ethics-and-society</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1109327714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer263328283251082332"><b>**Check out the original review over at <a href='http://21stcenturyonceuponatime.blogspot.com.au/2014/11/quick-picks-warprize-by-elizabeth.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>21st Century Once Upon A Times</a>**</b><blockquote>'<i>"But he has claimed tribute."<br/><br/>(...) "What does he claim?" I took a step toward Xymund. Still, he did not turn. I looked around, but no one would meet my eyes.<br/><br/>At last, general Warren drew a breath. "You," he cleared his throat. "He claims you as tribute."<br/><br/>"Me?" My voice squeaked and sounded like it came from a distance.<br/><br/>Xymund did not turn. "As a slave."</i>'</blockquote><b>Would you sacrifice your freedom for peace?</b><br/><br/>That question tends to be the o</span>
  <span id="freeText263328283251082332" style="display:none"><b>**Check out the original review over at <a href="http://21stcenturyonceuponatime.blogspot.com.au/2014/11/quick-picks-warprize-by-elizabeth.html" rel="nofollow noopener">21st Century Once Upon A Times</a>**</b><blockquote>'<i>"But he has claimed tribute."<br><br>(...) "What does he claim?" I took a step toward Xymund. Still, he did not turn. I looked around, but no one would meet my eyes.<br><br>At last, general Warren drew a breath. "You," he cleared his throat. "He claims you as tribute."<br><br>"Me?" My voice squeaked and sounded like it came from a distance.<br><br>Xymund did not turn. "As a slave."</i>'</blockquote><b>Would you sacrifice your freedom for peace?</b><br><br>That question tends to be the one that lingers after you've read the final page and closed the book. Xylara's choice - to give up her freedom, her control over her own life - in order to save her people and work towards a lasting peace, is admirable to be sure. <br><br>This book's plot, filled with difficult choices and trials for its heroine, is centered around the strengths and limitations of females in antiquity, especially those that led lives among the ranks of the nobility.<br><br>I loved the gypsy feel of the Plains people. The rich culture, vocabulary, traditions...it came to life on the page! Xylara's relationship with them changes and strengthens as she begins to realise her own potential and what it really means to be free.<br><br><b>Freedom is a choice. It is not something that can be taken from you.</b><br><br>On a funny note, every time they referred to Xylara as the 'tribute' the Warlord was demanding, I kept having visions of Xylara emerging from a crowd of villagers and staring defiantly at the Warlord, saying: <br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/volunteer%20as%20tribute" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416308857ra/11934080.gif" alt="volunteer as tribute photo: I Volunteer As Tribute cd756a14.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Although Xylara acts more like Prim/Peter than Katniss. She's a healer and - although badass - doesn't know how to fight, hunt or use a bow. <br><br>So...she's basically Katniss' less moody twin sister who smiles more (no offense, Katniss!)<br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/hunger%20games" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1416308857ra/11934081.gif" alt="hunger games photo: tumblr_m1hck2vT271qjlto9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Overall, it was an amazing read - one I'd definitely recommend :)<br><br><br></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4MdB7tQLh92sLCkJFG+fei+CObSnYGSxd7DRYz0Rytc+2JE9OeF6NrrO4yHDgmQ6P00Gjlpy6Mc3B7vYYiUt+g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8HSWpXi/bWR7glO9NLvI7YryMWxogDTRBgc0Hlk20jUua0Z2lVWQj21gmZXjVjOtmj0OVpWSuKdGsF6lBgI1GA==')})
  }

Monstrous creatures and deadly mysteries wait out here. Lucky for the people she serves, Shea’s not exactly sane. As a pathfinder, it’s her job to face what others fear and find the safest route through the wilderness. It’s not an easy job, but she’s the best at what she does.\n\nWhen the people she serves betray her into servitude to the Trateri, a barbarian horde sweeping through the Lowlands intent on conquest, Shea relies on her wits and skill to escape, disguising herself as a boy to hide from the Warlord, a man as dangerous as he is compelling.\n\nAfter being mistaken as a Trateri scout during her escape, Shea finds herself forced to choose between the life she led and the possibilities of a new one.   <span id="freeText1368440836256252793" style="display:none"><i>Librarian Note: There is more than one author in the GoodReads database with this name.</i> <br /><br />Elizabeth A. Vaughan is the author of the Chronicles of the Warlands, a fantasy romance trilogy from Tor Books: Warprize (her first novel), Warsworn, and Warlord..<br /><br />She's always loved fantasy and science fiction, and has been a fantasy role-player since 1981. By day, Beth's secret identity is that of a lawyer, practicing in the area of bankruptcy and financial matters, a role she has maintained since 1985.<br /><br />Beth is owned by three cats, and lives in the Northwest Territory, on the outskirts of the Black Swamp, along Mad Anthony's Trail on the banks of the Maumee River.</span>

Now a warrior-priestess, Snowfall, stands before Simus, who dares to speak of peace, of reconciliation. Her knives are sharp, her tattoos alluring, and her cool grey eyes can look through Simus and see…everything.  Now Simus and Snowfall must solve the mystery of the pillar of white light, and protect their people from all the destruction and chaos it brings. Snowfall fights for her place beside Simus, despite resistance from friend and foe.  The warrior-priests have abused their power for many years. Can Simus face the challenge of trusting Snowfall with his honor?
